                             ===Evaluation Report===                                                                                                                                                             
                             # Evaluation Report                                                                                                                                                                 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Summary                                                                                                                                                                          
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             A Jazzer fuzzing run against the Apache POI `POIFSDump` utility triggered a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception indicating a file path traversal. The sanitizer                 
                             detected that a constructed file path contains `..` segments leading outside the intended output directory.                                                                         
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Description                                                                                                                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             - Issue overview                                                                                                                                                                    
                               During fuzzing of the `POIPOIFSDumpFuzzer` harness, the call into `org.apache.poi.poifs.dev.POIFSDump.dump` led to a file path containing                                         
                             `../../../../jazzer-traversal`. The Jazzer `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer flagged this as a critical security issue and threw an exception.                                          
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             - Vulnerability type                                                                                                                                                                
                               This is a file path traversal vulnerability: untrusted or malformed entry names allow escaping the intended output directory.                                                     
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             - Key observations                                                                                                                                                                  
                                The exception originates in `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal.check` when verifying the first argument of a filewriting API.                          
                                The path under test (`/tmp/expander-tmp/q/r/s/t/input.bin_dump/Root Entry/../../../../jazzer-traversal`) contains upward directory hops that escape the target                 
                             base.                                                                                                                                                                               
                                The fuzzer harness (`POIPOIFSDumpFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`) is invoking `POIFSDump.main`/`.dump`, which in turn writes dump files based on POIFS entries.                      
                                No direct rootcause code is in the harness; it simply feeds arbitrary data into POIs dump routine.                                                                            
                                The sanitizers hook (`pathFirstArgHook`) flags each filecreation call, enforcing traversal checks.                                                                            
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             - Areas for investigation                                                                                                                                                           
                               1. The pathbuilding and fileoutput logic in `org.apache.poi.poifs.dev.POIFSDump` (and related POIFS modules) to see how entry names are translated into                         
                             filesystem paths.                                                                                                                                                                   
                               2. Any normalization or sanitization of POIFS entry names before use in file I/O.                                                                                                 
                               3. The interaction between POIs dump code and the underlying Java I/O APIs that accept the target path argument.                                                                 
                               4. Additional POI utilities or extractors that perform similar entrytofile mappings, to assess whether they share the same behavior.                                            
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Initial Issue Log                                                                                                                                                                
                             Here is the initial issue log of the codebase:

                             ## Fix Strategy                                                                                                                                                                     
                             <fix_strategy>                                                                                                                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             1. RootCause Analysis and Impact                                                                                                                                                   
                                - The traversal stems from using raw POIFS entry names (via `entry.getName()` or `node.getName().trim()`) directly as path components. Malicious entry names can                 
                             include .. or path separators, causing the constructed `File` or `Path` to escape the intended `parent` directory.                                                                
                                - We must preserve the recursive traversal and dump semantics: iterate over `DirectoryEntry` and `DocumentNode`, create subdirectories, write document bytes.                    
                             Only the way we turn entry names into filesystem names changes.                                                                                                                     
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             2. Protection Mechanism                                                                                                                                                             
                                - Introduce a sanitization step for any POIFS entry name before using it in file I/O. This step will:                                                                            
                                  a. Trim whitespace.                                                                                                                                                            
                                  b. Replace any forward/back-slash characters with a safe character (e.g. _).                                                                                                 
                                  c. Collapse or reject lone . and .. names.                                                                                                                                 
                                  d. Optionally check the final normalized path stays under `parent`.                                                                                                            
                                - After sanitization, verify via Java NIO that the normalized `childPath` starts with the normalized `parent` path; if not, abort with an `IOException`. This                    
                             second check guards against any edge cases in sanitization logic.                                                                                                                   
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             3. Implementation Steps                                                                                                                                                             
                                a. In `POIFSDump.java`, add a private helper:                                                                                                                                    
                                   ```                                                                                                                                                                           
                                   private static String sanitizeEntryName(String raw) throws IOException {                                                                                                      
                                       String name = raw.trim();                                                                                                                                                 
                                       // Replace slashes and back-slashes with underscore                                                                                                                       
                                       name = name.replaceAll("[/\\\\]+", "_");                                                                                                                                  
                                       if (name.isEmpty()) {                                                                                                                                                     
                                           throw new IOException("Invalid entry name (empty after sanitization): '" + raw + "'");                                                                                
                                       }                                                                                                                                                                         
                                       // Disallow "." and ".." as final names; map to safe identifiers                                                                                                          
                                       if (name.equals(".") || name.equals("..")) {                                                                                                                              
                                           name = "_" + name;                                                                                                                                                    
                                       }                                                                                                                                                                         
                                       return name;                                                                                                                                                              
                                   }                                                                                                                                                                             
                                   ```                                                                                                                                                                           
                                b. Replace all uses of `entry.getName()` or `node.getName().trim()` when constructing files/directories:                                                                         
                                   - For `DocumentNode` output (around line 108):                                                                                                                                
                                     ```                                                                                                                                                                         
                                     String rawName = node.getName();                                                                                                                                            
                                     String safeName = sanitizeEntryName(rawName);                                                                                                                               
                                     Path childPath = parent.toPath().resolve(safeName).toAbsolutePath().normalize();                                                                                            
                                     Path parentAbs = parent.toPath().toAbsolutePath().normalize();                                                                                                              
                                     if (!childPath.startsWith(parentAbs)) {                                                                                                                                     
                                         throw new IOException("Entry name leads outside target directory: '" + rawName + "'");                                                                                  
                                     }                                                                                                                                                                           
                                     try (OutputStream out = Files.newOutputStream(childPath)) {                                                                                                                 
                                         out.write(bytes);                                                                                                                                                       
                                     }                                                                                                                                                                           
                                     ```                                                                                                                                                                         
                                   - For `DirectoryEntry` recursion (around line 113):                                                                                                                           
                                     ```                                                                                                                                                                         
                                     String rawName = entry.getName();                                                                                                                                           
                                     String safeName = sanitizeEntryName(rawName);                                                                                                                               
                                     Path dirPath = parent.toPath().resolve(safeName).toAbsolutePath().normalize();                                                                                              
                                     Path parentAbs = parent.toPath().toAbsolutePath().normalize();                                                                                                              
                                     if (!dirPath.startsWith(parentAbs)) {                                                                                                                                       
                                         throw new IOException("Entry name leads outside target directory: '" + rawName + "'");                                                                                  
                                     }                                                                                                                                                                           
                                     File dirFile = dirPath.toFile();                                                                                                                                            
                                     if (!dirFile.exists() && !dirFile.mkdirs()) {                                                                                                                               
                                         throw new IOException("Could not create directory " + dirFile);                                                                                                         
                                     }                                                                                                                                                                           
                                     dump((DirectoryEntry)entry, dirFile);                                                                                                                                       
                                     ```                                                                                                                                                                         
                                c. (Optional) Apply the same sanitization to the toplevel `root.getName()` when creating the first subdirectory in `main()`. This ensures consistent handling                   
                             if the POIFS root name is non-standard.                                                                                                                                             
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             4. Preservation of Existing Functionality                                                                                                                                           
                                - When entry names are well-formed (no /, \, ..), `sanitizeEntryName` yields the original name, so all normal dumps behave identically.                                    
                                - The recursive dumping logic, directory structure, and byte output remain unchanged aside from the namesanitization layer.                                                     
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             5. Addressing the Security Report                                                                                                                                                   
                                - By sanitizing dangerous characters and rejecting/trapping names that would cause path traversal, the sanitizer in Jazzer will no longer see any `..` segments                  
                             in the first argument to `Files.newOutputStream` or directory creation APIs. The critical `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception for FilePathTraversal will thus                   
                             be prevented.                                                                                                                                                                       
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             6. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation                                                                                                                                            
                                - Tests or users expecting literal POIFS entry names containing slashes/back-slashes will see `_` instead. Such cases are extremely rare since POIFS entries                     
                             typically follow simple naming conventions.                                                                                                                                         
                                - If an entry name fully normalizes to an empty string, we throw an `IOException`. This is appropriate: entries without usable names cannot be dumped.                           
                                - The final pathstart check via `childPath.startsWith(parentAbs)` provides defenseindepth against any future edgecase bypasses in regex sanitization.                        
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             7. References and Precedent                                                                                                                                                         
                                - This pattern (sanitizing entry names + verifying normalized path prefixes) is recommended in security guidelines whenever untrusted or externally supplied                     
                             names map to filesystem paths.                                                                                                                                                      
                                - No changes are made to external libraries, harness code, or testsonly to the POIFSDump implementation, and all existing test suites should pass unaltered.                    
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             8. Conclusion                                                                                                                                                                       
                                - This fix strategy isolates the vulnerability at its source, preserves existing behavior for benign inputs, and ensures that no crafted POIFS entry can write                   
                             or create files outside the intended dump directory.                                                                                                                                
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             </fix_strategy>                                                                                                                                                                     
                             ===Evaluation End===

                             ===Evaluation Report===                                                                                                                                                             
                             # Evaluation Report                                                                                                                                                                 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Summary                                                                                                                                                                          
                             A Jazzer fuzzing run against Apache POIs `POIFSDump` tool triggered a critical security finding: a file path traversal vulnerability when processing crafted POIFS                 
                             entries named with ../../ sequences. In response, a candidate patch was introduced that trims and sanitizes entry names, replaces path separators with                            
                             underscores, resolves and normalizes target paths, and enforces that no resolved path escapes the intended dump directory. After applying the patch, the build                      
                             failed with multiple cannot find symbol: class Path errors in `POIFSDump.java`, indicating missing imports or incorrect Java API usage.                                           
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Description                                                                                                                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             Initial issue                                                                                                                                                                       
                             - During a Jazzer fuzzing session, the fuzzer passed an entry name containing Root Entry/../../../../jazzer-traversal to `POIFSDump`.                                             
                             - The Jazzer runtime flagged this as a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path traversal`, showing that untrusted entry names allowed writes outside the intended                   
                             dump directory (`/tmp//output/q/r/s/t/input.bin_dump/Root Entry/../../../../jazzer-traversal`).                                                                                    
                             - The stack trace pinpointed the failure in a sanitizer hook (`FilePathTraversal.pathFirstArgHook`) and in `POIFSDump.dump()`, which was creating files or                          
                             directories directly from entry names.                                                                                                                                              
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             Patch attempt                                                                                                                                                                       
                             - The patch modifies two main code regions in `POIFSDump.java`:                                                                                                                     
                               1. At the point where the top-level root directory is established, the code now:                                                                                                  
                                  - Retrieves `rawRootName` from `root.getName()`.                                                                                                                               
                                  - Applies `trim()` and a regex replace to convert any slash or backslash sequences into underscores, yielding `safeRootName`.                                                  
                                  - Rejects empty or purely ./.. names or prefixes them with _.                                                                                                            
                                  - Uses `dumpDir.toPath().resolve(safeRootName).toAbsolutePath().normalize()` to get `rootPath`, checks that it starts with the absolute normalized `dumpDir`                   
                             path, and throws if it does not.                                                                                                                                                    
                                  - Constructs a `File` from `rootPath` and attempts to `mkdirs()`.                                                                                                              
                               2. In recursive dumping of POIFS entries:                                                                                                                                         
                                  - For document entries, transforms `node.getName()` into `safeName` similarly, resolves it against `parent.toPath()`, normalizes, checks prefix containment,                   
                             and writes the document bytes there.                                                                                                                                                
                                  - For subdirectories, applies the same sanitization and containment checks before creating the directory and recursing.                                                        
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             Patch result                                                                                                                                                                        
                             - Applying the patch caused compilation to fail in `poi/poi/src/main/java/org/apache/poi/poifs/dev/POIFSDump.java`: every use of `Path` and related calls                           
                             (`toPath()`, `normalize()`, etc.) could not be resolved because `java.nio.file.Path` was not imported.                                                                              
                             - The build log reports six cannot find symbol: class Path errors, all located in `POIFSDump.java`.                                                                               
                             - Other modules compiled with warnings but no errors; the problem is isolated to missing references in `POIFSDump`.                                                                 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             Areas for further investigation                                                                                                                                                     
                             1. The imports and Java version compatibility in `POIFSDump.java`: ensure `import java.nio.file.Path; import java.nio.file.Paths;` (and possibly                                    
                             `java.nio.file.Files`) are present and that the project is targeting Java 7+ where NIO.2 is available.                                                                              
                             2. Whether similar sanitization or pathnormalization logic is needed in other POI tools that write files from entry names.                                                         
                             3. The build configuration for the `poi` module: confirm source and target compatibility levels and check for any enforcement that might omit NIO imports.                          
                             4. Potentially overlooked code paths in `POIFSDump` (e.g., error reporting or alternative I/O calls) where entry names are used directly.                                           
                             5. Harmonization of this patch with the rest of the POI coding style and exceptionhandling practices.

                             ## Fix Strategy                                                                                                                                                                     
                             <fix_strategy>                                                                                                                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             1. Root Cause Analysis                                                                                                                                                              
                                - The compilation errors in `POIFSDump.java` (cannot find symbol: class Path) are due to missing import of `java.nio.file.Path`. Although `Files` and `Paths`                  
                             are imported, the codes use of `Path` as a type in the sanitization logic is unresolved. Java will not infer missing imports for types referenced explicitly.                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             2. Critical Logic Preservation                                                                                                                                                      
                                - The sanitization and pathnormalization logic introduced in the last patch (trimming, replacing separators, rejecting empty/./.. names, resolving to                       
                             absolute paths, normalizing, containment checks) is essential to prevent file path traversal. We must reapply that patch in full, without alteration, so that we do                 
                             not regress the security fix.                                                                                                                                                       
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             3. Fix Steps                                                                                                                                                                        
                                A. Reapply the previous sanitization patch to `POIFSDump.java` (as provided in the last patch attempt), ensuring that all added uses of `Path` remain intact.                    
                                B. In the import section of `POIFSDump.java`, add the missing import for `java.nio.file.Path`. Specifically, modify the imports at the top of the file to                        
                             include:                                                                                                                                                                            
                                   ```                                                                                                                                                                           
                                   import java.nio.file.Path;                                                                                                                                                    
                                   import java.nio.file.Files;                                                                                                                                                   
                                   import java.nio.file.Paths;                                                                                                                                                   
                                   ```                                                                                                                                                                           
                                   so that the code references to `Path`, `Files`, and `Paths` resolve correctly.                                                                                                
                                C. No changes to build scripts, harness, tests, or external dependencies are required, because the POI Gradle settings target Java 9 (or above), where                           
                             `java.nio.file` is available.                                                                                                                                                       
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             4. Justification                                                                                                                                                                    
                                - Adding the single `Path` import fixes all six cannot find symbol errors without risk of altering existing logic.                                                             
                                - The sanitization logic remains untouched and continues to enforce that no entry escapes the dump directory, preserving the security patch.                                     
                                - This is a minimal change, avoiding broader codebase impacts or style violations (no wildcard imports; keeping discrete NIO imports).                                           
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             5. Potential Side Effects & Mitigation                                                                                                                                              
                                - No side effects: `java.nio.file.Path` is part of the JDK standard library on Java 7+ and is already available to the module.                                                   
                                - Code style: the import block ordering should follow project conventions (sorted lexically or grouped with other `java.nio.file` imports).                                      
                                - Build configuration remains unchanged; no further errors are expected.                                                                                                         
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             6. References                                                                                                                                                                       
                                - Existing import usage of `Files.newInputStream(Paths.get(...))` in lines 6869 demonstrates that the module already relies on NIO.2 APIs.                                      
                                - Gradles `sourceCompatibility = 1.9` ensures NIO.2 API availability.

                             ===Evaluation Report===                                                                                                                                                             
                             # Evaluation Report                                                                                                                                                                 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Summary                                                                                                                                                                          
                             The codebase under test (Apache POIs POIFSDump tool) triggers a Jazzer security exception for file path traversal when processing fuzzer-generated inputs. The                     
                             initial report shows `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path traversal` raised by `FilePathTraversal.check`, indicating unvalidated file paths are used downstream                  
                             in `POIFSDump.dump`. A minimal patch was appliedadding an import for `java.nio.file.Path`but the same exception continues to occur at the corresponding locations                 
                             in `POIFSDump.dump` and `POIFSDump.main`. The patch did not resolve the traversal detection and the crash remains.                                                                  
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Description                                                                                                                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             Initial Issue                                                                                                                                                                       
                             - Exception: `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path traversal`                                                                                    
                             - Crashing input path:                                                                                                                                                              
                               `/tmp/expander-tmp*/output/q/r/s/t/input.bin_dump/Root Entry/../../../../jazzer-traversal`                                                                                        
                             - Stack trace highlights the failure in:                                                                                                                                            
                               - `FilePathTraversal.check`  `FilePathTraversal.checkPath`  `FilePathTraversal.pathFirstArgHook`                                                                                
                               - `org.apache.poi.poifs.dev.POIFSDump.dump(POIFSDump.java:108)`                                                                                                                   
                               - `org.apache.poi.poifs.dev.POIFSDump.main(POIFSDump.java:80)`                                                                                                                    
                               - Entry point from `POIPOIFSDumpFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`                                                                                                                        
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             Key Observations                                                                                                                                                                    
                             - The fuzzer harness (`POIPOIFSDumpFuzzer`) invokes `POIFSDump.main` with crafted input files.                                                                                      
                             - Within `POIFSDump.dump`, file or directory names derived from POIFS entries are concatenated into output paths without normalization or sanitization.                             
                             - Jazzers `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer intercepts filewriting methods and flags relative paths (`../../..`) that escape intended directories.                                    
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             Patch Attempt                                                                                                                                                                       
                             - File modified: `poi/src/main/java/org/apache/poi/poifs/dev/POIFSDump.java`                                                                                                        
                             - Change summary: added an unused import                                                                                                                                            
                                 ```diff                                                                                                                                                                         
                                  import java.nio.file.Files;                                                                                                                                                    
                             +    import java.nio.file.Path;                                                                                                                                                     
                                  import java.nio.file.Paths;                                                                                                                                                    
                                 ```                                                                                                                                                                             
                             - No changes to the logic in `dump(...)` or `main(...)`.                                                                                                                            
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             Patch Result                                                                                                                                                                        
                             - After recompilation the same exception reappears, now reporting line numbers shifted by one:                                                                                      
                               - `POIFSDump.dump(POIFSDump.java:109)`                                                                                                                                            
                               - `POIFSDump.main(POIFSDump.java:81)`                                                                                                                                             
                             - The traversal path and Jazzer stack trace remain effectively identical, confirming the import-only patch did not alter path handling.                                             
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             Areas for Further Investigation                                                                                                                                                     
                             - The implementation of `POIFSDump.dump` where entry names and directory names are joined to form output paths.                                                                     
                             - Calls to `new OutputStream` or `Files` APIs in `dump(...)` that accept unvalidated path strings.                                                                                  
                             - The logic in `POIFSDump.main` that sets up the output directory and invokes `dump`.                                                                                               
                             - Any utility methods within the POIFS dev package that perform path concatenation or directory creation.                                                                           
                             - How POIFS entry names are sanitized (or not) before being used in file-system operations.

                             ## Fix Strategy                                                                                                                                                                     
                             <fix_strategy>                                                                                                                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             1. Root Cause and Affected Code                                                                                                                                                     
                                - The methods in `POIFSDump` directly concatenate POIFS entry names (and `root.getName()`) into file-system paths without any sanitization or validation.                        
                             Malicious entry names containing "../" or path separators allow filewrite calls to escape the intended dump directory, triggering Jazzers `FilePathTraversal`                   
                             sanitizer.                                                                                                                                                                          
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             2. Preservation of Existing Logic                                                                                                                                                   
                                - All existing loops, recursion, and use of `Files.newOutputStream` remain unchanged, ensuring the dump functionality (writing documents and creating                            
                             directories) is intact for benign inputs.                                                                                                                                           
                                - We do **not** modify harness code, test code, or external libraries. Only `POIFSDump.java` is patched.                                                                         
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             3. Strategy for Sanitizing Entry Names                                                                                                                                              
                                a. Introduce a private helper in `POIFSDump` to canonicalize/sanitize any entry name before using it in a file-system path:                                                      
                                   ```java                                                                                                                                                                       
                                   private static String sanitizeEntryName(String name) {                                                                                                                        
                                       if (name == null) {                                                                                                                                                       
                                           return "_";                                                                                                                                                           
                                       }                                                                                                                                                                         
                                       // 1) Replace path separators (/ or \) with underscore                                                                                                                
                                       // 2) Collapse any .. sequences into a single underscore                                                                                                                
                                       // 3) Replace other invalid filename chars with underscore                                                                                                                
                                       String safe = name.replaceAll("[/\\\\]+", "_")                                                                                                                            
                                                         .replaceAll("\\.\\.+", "_")                                                                                                                             
                                                         .replaceAll("[:*?\"<>|]", "_")                                                                                                                          
                                                         .trim();                                                                                                                                                
                                       return safe.isEmpty() ? "_" : safe;                                                                                                                                       
                                   }                                                                                                                                                                             
                                   ```                                                                                                                                                                           
                                b. For **each** file or directory creation/IO call, apply `sanitizeEntryName(...)` to the raw name before resolving or constructing a `File`/`Path`.                             
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             4. Validation via Normalization                                                                                                                                                     
                                - After resolving the sanitized name against the intended parent directory, normalize the resulting `Path`, then verify `normalizedPath.startsWith(parentDir)`.                  
                             If it does not, treat it as a fatal error (`IOException`) to avoid unexpected writing outside the dump tree.                                                                        
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             5. Patching Points in `POIFSDump.java`                                                                                                                                              
                                a. In `main(...)`, replace:                                                                                                                                                      
                                   ```java                                                                                                                                                                       
                                   File file = new File(dumpDir, root.getName());                                                                                                                                
                                   ```                                                                                                                                                                           
                                   with:                                                                                                                                                                         
                                   ```java                                                                                                                                                                       
                                   String rootNameSafe = sanitizeEntryName(root.getName());                                                                                                                      
                                   Path rootPath = dumpDir.toPath().resolve(rootNameSafe).normalize();                                                                                                           
                                   if (!rootPath.startsWith(dumpDir.toPath())) {                                                                                                                                 
                                       throw new IOException("Invalid POIFS root name: " + root.getName());                                                                                                      
                                   }                                                                                                                                                                             
                                   File file = rootPath.toFile();                                                                                                                                                
                                   ```                                                                                                                                                                           
                                b. In `dump(DirectoryEntry root, File parent)`, for the documentwriting branch:                                                                                                 
                                   ```java                                                                                                                                                                       
                                   String raw = node.getName().trim();                                                                                                                                           
                                   String safe = sanitizeEntryName(raw);                                                                                                                                         
                                   Path outPath = parent.toPath().resolve(safe).normalize();                                                                                                                     
                                   if (!outPath.startsWith(parent.toPath())) {                                                                                                                                   
                                       throw new IOException("Invalid entry name: " + raw);                                                                                                                      
                                   }                                                                                                                                                                             
                                   try (OutputStream out = Files.newOutputStream(outPath)) {                                                                                                                     
                                       out.write(bytes);                                                                                                                                                         
                                   }                                                                                                                                                                             
                                   ```                                                                                                                                                                           
                                   And for directories:                                                                                                                                                          
                                   ```java                                                                                                                                                                       
                                   String raw = entry.getName();                                                                                                                                                 
                                   String safe = sanitizeEntryName(raw);                                                                                                                                         
                                   Path dirPath = parent.toPath().resolve(safe).normalize();                                                                                                                     
                                   if (!dirPath.startsWith(parent.toPath())) {                                                                                                                                   
                                       throw new IOException("Invalid entry name: " + raw);                                                                                                                      
                                   }                                                                                                                                                                             
                                   File file = dirPath.toFile();                                                                                                                                                 
                                   if (!file.exists() && !file.mkdirs()) {                                                                                                                                       
                                       throw new IOException("Could not create directory " + file);                                                                                                              
                                   }                                                                                                                                                                             
                                   dump((DirectoryEntry)entry, file);                                                                                                                                            
                                   ```                                                                                                                                                                           
                                c. In `dump(POIFSFileSystem fs, int startBlock, String name, File parent)`, replace:                                                                                             
                                   ```java                                                                                                                                                                       
                                   File file = new File(parent, name);                                                                                                                                           
                                   ```                                                                                                                                                                           
                                   with:                                                                                                                                                                         
                                   ```java                                                                                                                                                                       
                                   String safe = sanitizeEntryName(name);                                                                                                                                        
                                   Path filePath = parent.toPath().resolve(safe).normalize();                                                                                                                    
                                   if (!filePath.startsWith(parent.toPath())) {                                                                                                                                  
                                       throw new IOException("Invalid entry name: " + name);                                                                                                                     
                                   }                                                                                                                                                                             
                                   if (!Files.isDirectory(filePath.getParent())) {                                                                                                                               
                                       Files.createDirectories(filePath.getParent());                                                                                                                            
                                   }                                                                                                                                                                             
                                   try (OutputStream out = Files.newOutputStream(filePath)) {                                                                                                                    
                                       ...                                                                                                                                                                       
                                   }                                                                                                                                                                             
                                   ```                                                                                                                                                                           
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             6. Justification                                                                                                                                                                    
                                - Sanitizing entry names at every join point guarantees no ../ or embedded separators remain, preventing any pathtraversal vector.                                            
                                - Path normalization and prefixchecking provide a second line of defenseany incorrectly sanitized or unexpected name causing an escape is caught and aborted.                  
                                - The dump logic (recursion, document serialization, directory creation) remains intact for valid entries.                                                                       
                                - No external dependencies or test/harness code are modified, satisfying fuzzing and CI requirements.                                                                            
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             7. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation                                                                                                                                            
                                - Legitimate POIFS entry names that include unusual characters or multiple dots will be remapped (e.g., ..folder  _folder), possibly altering the ondisk                  
                             dump structure. This is acceptable since these characters are rarely critical and existing tools already sanitize filenames routinely.                                              
                                - If an entry name sanitizes to an empty string, we map it to _ to avoid creating unnamed files.                                                                               
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             8. References                                                                                                                                                                       
                                - Similar filenamesanitization in `poi-ooxml/src/.../Util.sanitizeFilename(String)` replaces invalid chars with underscores. We extend it to remove path                        
                             separators and .. sequences.                                                                                                                                                      
                                - Normalizationplusprefixcheck is a wellknown pattern to prevent directoryescape attacks in fileupload handlers.                                                           
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             </fix_strategy>

                             No tests found
